         ++m_cursor;\n                return { TokenType::RParen, \")\", m_cursor - 1 };\n            case '\"':\n                return lex_phrase();\n            default:\n                break;\n        }\n\n        // Word or reserved keyword\n        if (std::isalnum(static_cast<unsigned char>(ch)) || ch == '_' || ch == '-')\n        {\n            auto word = read_while([](unsigned char c) {\n                return std::isalnum(c) || c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';\n            });\n\n            const auto lower = to_lower(word);\n            if (lower == \"and\")\n                return { TokenType::And, word, m_cursor - word.size() };\n            if (lower == \"or\")\n                return { TokenType::Or, word, m_cursor - word.size() };\n            if (lower == \"not\")\n                return { TokenType::Not, word, m_cursor - word.size() };\n\n            return { TokenType::Word, word, m_cursor - word.size() };\n        }\n\n        throw ParseError { std::string { \"Invalid character '\" } + ch + \"'\", m_cursor };\n    }\n\n    Token lex_phrase()\n    {\n        const std::size_t start_pos = m_cursor;\n        ++m_cursor; // skip opening quote\n\n        std::ostringstream oss;\n        bool escaped = false;\n\n        while (m_cursor < m_input.size())\n        {\n            char ch = m_input[m_cursor++];\n            if (escaped)\n            {\n                // Accept common escape sequences or keep char as is\n                switch (ch)\n                {\n                    case '\"':  oss << '\"'; break;\n                    case '\\\\': oss << '\\\\'; break;\n                    case 'n':  oss << '\\n'; break;\n                    case 't':  oss << '\\t'; break;\n                    default:   oss << ch;  break;\n                }\n                escaped = false;\n            }\n            else if (ch == '\\\\')\n            {\n                escaped = true;\n            }\n            else if (ch == '\"')\n            {\n                // End of phrase\n                return { TokenType::Phrase, oss.str(), start_pos };\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                oss << ch;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Reached end-of-input without closing quote\n        throw ParseError { \"Unterminated string literal\", start_pos };\n    }\n\n    static std::string to_lower(std::string_view sv)\n    {\n        std::string out;\n        out.reserve(sv.size());\n        std::transform(sv.begin(), sv.end(), std::back_inserter(out),\n                       [](unsigned char c) { return static_cast<char>(std::tolower(c)); });\n        return out;\n    }\n};\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nstruct \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nclass }\n        return node;\n    }\n\n    // Intermediate level: AND (implicit or explicit)\n    NodePtr parse_and()\n    {\n        auto node = parse_unary();\n\n        while (true)\n        {\n            if (match(TokenType::And))\n            {\n                auto rhs = parse_unary();\n                node     = std::make_unique<QueryNode>(And { std::move(node), std::move(rhs) });\n            }\n            // Implicit AND: two consecutive terms / groups\n            else if (peek_any({ TokenType::Word, TokenType::Phrase, TokenType::LParen, TokenType::Not }))\n            {\n The service\n * maintains an in-memory inverted index for efficient full-text search operations.\n *\n * This refactoring consolidates search logic previously scattered across:\n *   - module_18.cpp (search query parser)\n *   - module_41.cpp (search service and ranking)\n *   - module_61.cpp (search DSL and SQL translation)\n *\n * Copyright \u00a9 2024 IntraLedger\n */\n\n#ifndef INTRALEDGER_SEARCH_SERVICE_H\n#define INTRALEDGER_SEARCH_SERVICE_H\n\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <cctype>\n#include <map>\n#include <mutex>\n#include <shared_mutex>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_map>\n#include <unordered_set>\n#include <vector>\n\nnamespace intraledger::search {\n\n/**\n * @class SearchService\n * @brief Centralized service for document indexing and search query processing\n *\n * The SearchService maintains an in-memory inverted index that maps tokens to\n * document IDs. It provides methods for indexing documents and executing search\n * queries against the indexed content.\n *\n * Thread-safety: All public methods are thread-safe for concurrent access.\n */\nclass SearchService {\npublic:\n    /**\n     * @brief Get the singleton instance of SearchService\n     * @return Reference to the global SearchService instance\n     */\n    static SearchService& instance();\n\n    /**\n     * @brief Index a document for full-text search\n     *\n     * Tokenizes the document content and adds it to the inverted index.\n     * If the document was previously indexed, the old index entries are\n     * replaced with new ones.\n     *\n     * @param documentId Unique identifier for the document\n     * @param documentContent The text content to be indexed\n     */\n    void indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent);\n\n    /**\n     * @brief Execute a search query against the indexed documents\n     *\n     * Tokenizes the search term and finds all documents containing\n     * the specified terms. Results are returned sorted by relevance\n     * (number of matching terms).\n     *\n     * @param searchTerm The search query string\n     * @return Vector of document IDs that match the query, sorted by relevance\n     */\n    std::vector<int> query(const std::string& searchTerm);\n\n    /**\n     * @brief Remove a document from the search index\n     * @param documentId The ID of the document to remove\n     */\n    void removeDocument(int documentId);\n\n    /**\n     * @brief Clear all indexed documents\n     */\n    void clearIndex();\n\n    /**\n     * @brief Get the number of indexed documents\n     * @return Count of unique documents in the index\n     */\n    std::size_t documentCount() const;\n\n    // Prevent copying and moving\n    SearchService(const SearchService&) = delete;\n    SearchService& operator=(const SearchService&) = delete;\n    SearchService(SearchService&&) = delete;\n    SearchService& operator=(SearchService&&) = delete;\n\nprivate:\n    SearchService() = default;\n    ~SearchService() = default;\n\n    /**\n     * @brief Tokenize text into searchable terms\n     *\n     * Splits text on whitespace and punctuation, converts to lowercase,\n     * and filters out very short tokens.\n     *\n     * @param text The text to tokenize\n     * @return Vector of normalized tokens\n     */\n    static std::vector<std::string> tokenize(const std::string& text);\n\n    /// Inverted index: token -> list of document IDs\n    std::map<std::string, std::vector<int>> invertedIndex;\n\n    /// Set of all indexed document IDs\n    std::unordered_set<int> indexedDocuments;\n\n    /// Mutex for thread-safe access to the inverted index\n    mutable std::shared_mutex indexMutex;\n};\n\n} // namespace intraledger::search\n\n#endif // INTRALEDGER_SEARCH_SERVICE_H\n",

It provides methods for indexing documents and executing search\n * queries against the indexed content.\n *\n * Thread-safety: All public methods are thread-safe for concurrent access.\n */\nclass SearchService {\npublic:\n    static SearchService& instance();\n    void indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent);\n    std::vector<int> query(const std::string& searchTerm);\n    void removeDocument(int documentId);\n    void clearIndex();\n    std::size_t documentCount() const;\n\nprivate:\n    SearchService() = default;\n    ~SearchService() = default;\n    static std::vector<std::string> tokenize(const std::string& text);\n\n    std::map<std::string, std::vector<int>> invertedIndex;\n    std::unordered_set<int> indexedDocuments;\n    mutable std::shared_mutex indexMutex;\n};\n```\n\n### SearchService Implementation (SearchService.cpp)\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/search/SearchService.cpp\n// Lines: 26-86\n\nvoid SearchService::indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent) {\n    std::vector<std::string> tokens = tokenize(documentContent);\n    std::unordered_set<std::string> uniqueTokens(tokens.begin(), tokens.end());\n\n    std::unique_lock<std::shared_mutex> lock(indexMutex);\n\n    // If document was previously indexed, remove old entries\n    if (indexedDocuments.count(documentId) > 0) {\n        for (auto& [token, docIds] : invertedIndex) {\n            auto it = std::find(docIds.begin(), docIds.end(), documentId);\n            if (it != docIds.end()) {\n                docIds.erase(it);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Add new index entries\n    for (const auto& token : uniqueTokens) {\n        auto& docIds = invertedIndex[token];\n        if (std::find(docIds.begin(), docIds.end(), documentId) == docIds.end()) {\n            docIds.push_back(documentId);\n        }\n    }\n\n    indexedDocuments.insert(documentId);\n}\n\nstd::vector<int> SearchService::query(const std::string& searchTerm) {\n    if (searchTerm.empty()) {\n        return {};\n    }\n\n    std::vector<std::string> tokens = tokenize(searchTerm);\n    if (tokens.empty()) {\n        return {};\n    }\n\n    std::unordered_map<int, std::size_t> scoreTable;\n    {\n        std::shared_lock<std::shared_mutex> lock(indexMutex);\n        for (const auto& token : tokens) {\n            auto it = invertedIndex.find(token);\n            if (it != invertedIndex.end()) {\n                for (int docId : it->second) {\n                    ++scoreTable[docId];\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    std::vector<std::pair<int, std::size_t>> ranked(scoreTable.begin(), scoreTable.end());\n    std::sort(ranked.begin(), ranked.end(),\n              [](const auto& a, const auto& b) { return a.second > b.second; });\n\n    std::vector<int> result;\n    result.reserve(ranked.size());\n    for (const auto& [docId, score] : ranked) {\n        result.push_back(docId);\n    }\n    return result;\n}\n```\n\n### Integration in module_18.cpp\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_18.cpp\n// Lines: 38, 562-579\n\n#include \"search/SearchService.h\"\n\n// ...\n\n/**\n * @brief Index a blog post document using the centralized SearchService\n */\nvoid indexBlogPost(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent)\n{\n    SearchService::instance().indexDocument(documentId, documentContent);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Query indexed documents using the centralized SearchService\n */\nstd::vector<int> searchBlogPosts(const std::string& searchTerm)\n{\n    return SearchService::instance().query(searchTerm);\n}\n```\n\n### Integration in module_41.cpp\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_41.cpp\n// Lines: 63-64, 506-517, 557-568\n\n// Include the intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().query(searchTerm);\n}\n```\n\n### Integration in module_61.cpp\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_61.cpp\n// Lines: 59-60, 628-645\n\n// Include the centralized SearchService for in-memory index operations\n#include \"search/SearchService.h\"\n\n// ...\n\nvoid indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent)\n{\n intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().query(searchTerm);\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### How the Components Interact\n\n1. **SearchService (Centralized Core)**: The new `SearchService` class in `src/search/` is a thread-safe singleton that manages an in-memory inverted index. It provides two primary methods:\n   - `indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent)` - Tokenizes content and adds it to the inverted index\n   - `query(const std::string& searchTerm)` - Searches the index and returns matching document IDs sorted by relevance\n\n2. **module_18.cpp (Query Parser)**: This module continues to provide boolean-aware query parsing for SQL generation, but now also exposes convenience functions (`indexBlogPost`, `searchBlogPosts`) that delegate to the centralized SearchService.\n\n3. **module_41.cpp (Search Subsystem)**: This module retains SQL-based search capabilities through `DatabaseSearchService` but now also integrates with the centralized SearchService for fast in-memory index operations via `searchIndex()` and `indexDocument()` methods.\n\n4. **module_61.cpp (Search DSL)**: This module retains SQL translation capabilities for complex field-scoped queries but now also provides `indexDocument()` and `queryIndex()` functions that use the centralized SearchService.\n\n### Architectural Pattern Used\n\n- **Singleton Pattern**: The `SearchService` uses the singleton pattern via `instance()` to ensure a single shared index across all modules\n- **Thread-Safe Design**: Uses `std::shared_mutex` for read-write locking to allow concurrent reads while ensuring exclusive writes\n- **Inverted Index**: Implements a classic inverted index data structure (`std::map<std::string, std::vector<int>>`) for efficient full-text search\n- **TF Scoring**: Documents are scored by term frequency (number of matching search terms) and returned in descending order of relevance\n\n### Dependencies and Relationships\n\n```\n It provides methods for indexing documents and executing search\n * queries against the indexed content.\n *\n * Thread-safety: All public methods are thread-safe for concurrent access.\n */\nclass SearchService {\npublic:\n    static SearchService& instance();\n    void indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent);\n    std::vector<int> query(const std::string& searchTerm);\n    void removeDocument(int documentId);\n    void clearIndex();\n    std::size_t documentCount() const;\n\nprivate:\n    SearchService() = default;\n    ~SearchService() = default;\n    static std::vector<std::string> tokenize(const std::string& text);\n\n    std::map<std::string, std::vector<int>> invertedIndex;\n    std::unordered_set<int> indexedDocuments;\n    mutable std::shared_mutex indexMutex;\n};\n```\n\n### SearchService Implementation (SearchService.cpp)\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/search/SearchService.cpp\n// Lines: 26-86\n\nvoid SearchService::indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent) {\n    std::vector<std::string> tokens = tokenize(documentContent);\n    std::unordered_set<std::string> uniqueTokens(tokens.begin(), tokens.end());\n\n    std::unique_lock<std::shared_mutex> lock(indexMutex);\n\n    // If document was previously indexed, remove old entries\n    if (indexedDocuments.count(documentId) > 0) {\n        for (auto& [token, docIds] : invertedIndex) {\n            auto it = std::find(docIds.begin(), docIds.end(), documentId);\n            if (it != docIds.end()) {\n                docIds.erase(it);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Add new index entries\n    for (const auto& token : uniqueTokens) {\n        auto& docIds = invertedIndex[token];\n        if (std::find(docIds.begin(), docIds.end(), documentId) == docIds.end()) {\n            docIds.push_back(documentId);\n        }\n    }\n\n    indexedDocuments.insert(documentId);\n}\n\nstd::vector<int> SearchService::query(const std::string& searchTerm) {\n    if (searchTerm.empty()) {\n        return {};\n    }\n\n    std::vector<std::string> tokens = tokenize(searchTerm);\n    if (tokens.empty()) {\n        return {};\n    }\n\n    std::unordered_map<int, std::size_t> scoreTable;\n    {\n        std::shared_lock<std::shared_mutex> lock(indexMutex);\n        for (const auto& token : tokens) {\n            auto it = invertedIndex.find(token);\n            if (it != invertedIndex.end()) {\n                for (int docId : it->second) {\n                    ++scoreTable[docId];\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    std::vector<std::pair<int, std::size_t>> ranked(scoreTable.begin(), scoreTable.end());\n    std::sort(ranked.begin(), ranked.end(),\n              [](const auto& a, const auto& b) { return a.second > b.second; });\n\n    std::vector<int> result;\n    result.reserve(ranked.size());\n    for (const auto& [docId, score] : ranked) {\n        result.push_back(docId);\n    }\n    return result;\n}\n```\n\n### Integration in module_18.cpp\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_18.cpp\n// Lines: 38, 562-579\n\n#include \"search/SearchService.h\"\n\n// ...\n\n/**\n * @brief Index a blog post document using the centralized SearchService\n */\nvoid indexBlogPost(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent)\n{\n    SearchService::instance().indexDocument(documentId, documentContent);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Query indexed documents using the centralized SearchService\n */\nstd::vector<int> searchBlogPosts(const std::string& searchTerm)\n{\n    return SearchService::instance().query(searchTerm);\n}\n```\n\n### Integration in module_41.cpp\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_41.cpp\n// Lines: 63-64, 506-517, 557-568\n\n// Include the centralized SearchService\n#include \"search/SearchService.h\"\n\n// In DatabaseSearchService class:\nstd::vector<int> searchIndex(const std::string& query)\n{\n    return intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().query(query);\n}\n\nvoid indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& content)\n{\n    intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().indexDocument(documentId, content);\n}\n\n// Convenience functions:\nvoid indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent)\n{\n    intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().indexDocument(documentId, documentContent);\n}\n\nstd::vector<int> queryDocuments(const std::string& searchTerm)\n{\n    return intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().query(searchTerm);\n}\n```\n\n### Integration in module_61.cpp\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_61.cpp\n// Lines: 59-60, 628-645\n\n// Include the centralized SearchService for in-memory index operations\n#include \"search/SearchService.h\"\n\n// ...\n\nvoid indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent)\n{\n    intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().indexDocument(documentId, documentContent);\n}\n\nstd::vector<int> queryIndex(const std::string& searchTerm)\n{\n    return intraledger::search::SearchService::instance().query(searchTerm);\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### How the Components Interact\n\n1. **SearchService (Centralized Core)**: The new `SearchService` class in `src/search/` is a thread-safe singleton that manages an in-memory inverted index. It provides two primary methods:\n   - `indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent)` - Tokenizes content and adds it to the inverted index\n   - `query(const std::string& searchTerm)` - Searches the index and returns matching document IDs sorted by relevance\n\n2. **module_18.cpp (Query Parser)**: This module continues to provide boolean-aware query parsing for SQL generation, but now also exposes convenience functions (`indexBlogPost`, `searchBlogPosts`) that delegate to the centralized SearchService.\n\n3. **module_41.cpp (Search Subsystem)**: This module retains SQL-based search capabilities through `DatabaseSearchService` but now also integrates with the centralized SearchService for fast in-memory index operations via `searchIndex()` and `indexDocument()` methods.\n\n4. **module_61.cpp (Search DSL)**: This module retains SQL translation capabilities for complex field-scoped queries but now also provides `indexDocument()` and `queryIndex()` functions that use the centralized SearchService.\n\n### Architectural Pattern Used\n\n- **Singleton Pattern**: The `SearchService` uses the singleton pattern via `instance()` to ensure a single shared index across all modules\n- **Thread-Safe Design**: Uses `std::shared_mutex` for read-write locking to allow concurrent reads while ensuring exclusive writes\n- **Inverted Index**: Implements a classic inverted index data structure (`std::map<std::string, std::vector<int>>`) for efficient full-text search\n- **TF Scoring**: Documents are scored by term frequency (number of matching search terms) and returned in descending order of relevance\n\n### Dependencies and Relationships\n\n```\n 4. WRITE /tmp/project_copy/src/search/SearchService.cpp
/**
 * @file SearchService.cpp
 * @brief Implementation of the centralized SearchService for IntraLedger BlogSuite
 *
 * This implementation consolidates search-related logic that was previously
 * scattered across multiple modules:
 *   - Tokenization logic from module_18.cpp and module_61.cpp
 *   - Inverted index management from module_41.cpp
 *   - Query processing and ranking
 *
 * Copyright © 2024 IntraLedger
 */

#include "SearchService.h"
#include <algorithm>
#include <cctype>
#include <unordered_map>

namespace intraledger::search {

SearchService& SearchService::instance() {
    static SearchService instance;
    return instance;
}

void SearchService::indexDocument(int documentId, const std::string& documentContent) {
    // Tokenize the document content
    std::vector<std::string> tokens = tokenize(documentContent);

    // Get unique tokens for this document
    std::unordered_set<std::string> uniqueTokens(tokens.begin(), tokens.end());

    std::unique_lock<std::shared_mutex> lock(indexMutex);

    // If document was previously indexed, remove old entries
    if (indexedDocuments.count(documentId) > 0) {
        for (auto& [token, docIds] : invertedIndex) {
            auto it = std::find(docIds.begin(), docIds.end(), documentId);
            if (it != docIds.end()) {
                docIds.erase(it);
            }
        }
    }

    // Add new index entries
    for (const auto& token : uniqueTokens) {
        auto& docIds = invertedIndex[token];
        if (std::find(docIds.begin(), docIds.end(), documentId) == docIds.end()) {
            docIds.push_back(documentId);
        }
    }

    // Track this document as indexed
    indexedDocuments.insert(documentId);
}

/*
 *  IntraLedger BlogSuite – Search Query Parser (Refactored)
 *
 *  File:        src/module_18.cpp
 *  Author:      IntraLedger Core Team
 *  Description: Implements a boolean-aware, phrase-capable search query parser
 *               that folds to a parametrized SQL WHERE fragment consumable
 *               by the Repository/ORM layer.  The parser recognises:
 *
 *                 • Logical AND, OR, NOT   (case-insensitive, symbolic &&, ||, !)
 *                 • Parenthesis for precedence grouping
 *                 • Double-quoted phrases
 *                 • Plain words with automatic wildcard suffix
 *
 *               The output is safe for prepared statements; parameters are
 *               emitted separately to avoid SQL-injection.

 *               Search indexing functionality has been consolidated into the
 *               centralized SearchService (src/search/SearchService.h).
 *               This module now delegates indexing operations to SearchService.

 *  Copyright © 2024 IntraLedger
 */

namespace detail
{
inline std::string to_lower(std::string_view sv)
{
    std::string out;
    out.reserve(sv.size());
    std::transform(sv.begin(), sv.end(), std::back_inserter(out),
                   [](unsigned char ch) { return static_cast<char>(std::tolower(ch)); });
    return out;
}

/**
 *  IntraLedger BlogSuite

 *  File:        src/module_41.cpp
 *  Author:      IntraLedger Engineering
 *
 *  Description:
 *      Core search subsystem responsible for parsing free-form user queries,
 *      translating them into safe SQL fragments understood by the ORM, executing
 *      the query, and finally scoring & highlighting the resulting documents.
 *
 *      The goal of this module is to keep search-related logic well‐encapsulated
 *      and agnostic to the underlying persistence implementation (MariaDB /
 *      PostgreSQL).  All DB interaction is performed through the generic
 *      `IArticleRepository` interface defined in the Repository layer.
 *
 *  REFACTORING NOTE:
 *      Core search indexing and query functionality has been consolidated into
 *      the centralized SearchService (src/search/SearchService.h).
 *      This module now uses the centralized SearchService for index-based queries
 *      while retaining SQL-based search capabilities for database queries.
 *
 *      Dependencies:
 *          – C++20 STL
 *          – fmt            (header-only; used for safe SQL construction)
 *          – utf8proc       (optional; compile-time flag SEARCH_UTF8_NORMALIZE)
 *          – spdlog         (header-only; logging)
 *
 *      Thread-safety:
 *          All public functions are thread-safe and may be accessed from the
 *          async job processor or regular request threads concurrently.  The
 *          service makes no global mutations and relies on immutable data
 *          structures as much as possible.

# Solution: cpp_web_blog_expert_040_cross_file_refactoring_expert_01

## Key Files Identified

### New Files Created
- /app/project/src/search/SearchService.h - Centralized search service header with `indexDocument` and `query` interface
- /app/project/src/search/SearchService.cpp - Implementation of the centralized SearchService with inverted index

### Modified Files
- /app/project/src/module_18.cpp - Search Query Parser - Updated to include and use SearchService
- /app/project/src/module_41.cpp - Core Search Subsystem - Updated to use centralized SearchService
- /app/project/src/module_61.cpp - Search DSL Parser & SQL Translation - Updated to use centralized SearchService

### Original Files Analyzed
- /app/project/src/module_18.cpp - Original search query parser with tokenizer, parser, and SQL emitter
- /app/project/src/module_41.cpp - Original search service with query parsing, ranking, and snippet extraction
- /app/project/src/module_61.cpp - Original search DSL with lexer, parser, AST, and SQL translator

#!/bin/bash
# Script to apply the SearchService refactoring changes
# Run this script with appropriate permissions to apply changes to /app/project

set -e

SOURCE_DIR="/logs/agent/project_changes"
TARGET_DIR="/app/project/src"

echo "Creating search directory..."
mkdir -p "$TARGET_DIR/search"

echo "Copying SearchService files..."
cp "$SOURCE_DIR/search/SearchService.h" "$TARGET_DIR/search/"
cp "$SOURCE_DIR/search/SearchService.cpp" "$TARGET_DIR/search/"

cp "$SOURCE_DIR/module_18.cpp" "$TARGET_DIR/"
cp "$SOURCE_DIR/module_41.cpp" "$TARGET_DIR/"
cp "$SOURCE_DIR/module_61.cpp" "$TARGET_DIR/"

ls -la "$TARGET_DIR/search/"
echo ""
